\fbox{y11}\quad \mathbb{T}_{1,1}^{(s)}(T_{1})=\left[ 0,\, 0,\, \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2} \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y12}\quad \mathbb{T}_{1,2}^{(s)}(T_{1})=\left[ \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2},\, 0,\, 0,\, \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2} \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y13}\quad \mathbb{T}_{1,3}^{(s)}(T_{1})=\left[ \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2},\, 0,\, 0 \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y14}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(s)}(T_{2})=\left[ \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\, - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\, 0,\, 0,\, 0,\, 0 \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y15}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(s)}(T_{2})=\left[ 0,\, 0,\, \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\, - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\, 0,\, 0 \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y16}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(s)}(T_{2})=\left[ 0,\, 0,\, 0,\, 0,\, \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\, - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y17}\quad \mathbb{M}_{2,1}^{(s)}(T_{2})=\left[ 0,\, 0,\, - \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2} \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y18}\quad \mathbb{M}_{2,2}^{(s)}(T_{2})=\left[ \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2},\, 0,\, 0,\, - \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2} \right]
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{y19}\quad \mathbb{M}_{2,3}^{(s)}(T_{2})=\left[ - \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2},\, \frac{i}{2},\, - \frac{i}{2},\, 0,\, 0 \right]
\end{dmath*}
\vspace{5mm}
